Yo, lets go. Here's a sampler platter  pick your flavor and we can dive deeper: ^ref-b5e0183e-1-0

---

###  **Algebra**

Solve for xx: ^ref-b5e0183e-7-0
(3x5)(x+2)=0(3x - 5)(x + 2) = 0  
 Solutions:  
x=53x = \frac{5}{3} or x=2x = -2

---

###  **Geometry**

Area of a circle: ^ref-b5e0183e-16-0
A=r2A = \pi r^2  
If r=4r = 4:  
A=42=16A = \pi \cdot 4^2 = 16\pi

---

###  **Statistics**

Mean of: [4,8,15,16,23,42][4, 8, 15, 16, 23, 42] ^ref-b5e0183e-25-0
=4+8+15+16+23+426=1086=18\mu = \frac{4 + 8 + 15 + 16 + 23 + 42}{6} = \frac{108}{6} = 18

---

###  **Calculus**

Derivative of f(x)=x2sin(x)f(x) = x^2 \sin(x): ^ref-b5e0183e-32-0
Use product rule:  
f(x)=2xsin(x)+x2cos(x)f'(x) = 2x \sin(x) + x^2 \cos(x)

---

###  **Linear Algebra**

Dot product of a=[1,2]\vec{a} = [1, 2] and b=[3,4]\vec{b} = [3, 4]: ^ref-b5e0183e-40-0
(1)(3)+(2)(4)=3+8=11(1)(3) + (2)(4) = 3 + 8 = 11

---

###  **Cool One: Eulers Identity**

ei+1=0{e}^{i\pi} + 1 = 0 ^ref-b5e0183e-47-0
Links:

- ee: exponential growth ^ref-b5e0183e-50-0
    
- ii: imaginary unit ^ref-b5e0183e-52-0
    
- \pi: circle constant ^ref-b5e0183e-54-0
    
- 1 and 0: identity elements ^ref-b5e0183e-56-0
    

---
